I have bi-weekly calls with our rep to discuss any issues we're having and to learn about new features coming down the pipeline. They also have a support email that our affiliates can reach out to if they're having any issues with the platform or need help navigating it. Our team is very lean so this support allows us to focus on other areas. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Nothing really comes to mind. I think our Director would say she wishes we paid a little less but that's mostly because we have such a small budget for tools and platforms. We paid less with our previous platform but you definitely get what you pay for and we're very happy with our decision to move to Partnerize. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4136468 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize solved two big problems for us. It lighted our load in terms of the number of emails we need to respond to. Most of the questions we get are related to the platform and we love that we can direct them to the Partnerize support email. The other problem it solved, which was the biggest, was around our payments. We were coordinating hundreds of payments to our affiliates each quarter which was a lot of work for us as well as our finance team. With Partnerize we're able to make one payment to them each month and they handle all aspects of payment with each of our affiliates. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle" 2.667z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="tag" data-container="body" title="Invitation from G2 on behalf of a seller or affiliate. This reviewer was offered a nominal incentive as thanks for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Review source: G2 invite on behalf of seller</div><div class="tag" title="This reviewer was offered a nominal incentive as thanks for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Incentivized Review</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-10"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2020-03-02" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2020-03-02">Mar 02, 2020</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/partnerize/reviews/partnerize-review-4136415"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Great Platform"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I've used Partnerize from both sides, publisher, and partner. Both are great. Reporting is robust, and the documentation is helpful. The Partnerize staff is always very kind, professional and quick to respond. The platform is easy to use and seems to be constantly evolving. There always seems to be new features right around the corner. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">There really isn't much to dislike about such a powerful platform. If I had to be nitpicky and choose something it would likely be something along the lines of the reporting. The more advanced reporting is somewhat limited when it comes to pivoting the data with certain attributes. You're only allowed to create report pivots with some of the standard attributes, not with custom data, like publisher references. Not the end of the world though. Simply exporting the data from the Partnerize platform and opening it in Excel will let you achieve the same thing. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4136415 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Partnerize:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">There are a lot of other affiliate platforms out there right now. Consider the documentation or them and how the support is. Partnerize is amazing at both of those and when you need support, for whatever reason, you'll be glad you chose Partnerize. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4136415 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">There are so many affiliate platforms available. But none gives the same hands-on approach that Partnerize does. I have monthly calls with our rep to go over new features or introductions to new clients, or even just going over report publisher-specific reports and something they noticed that I missed. I'm able to reach more publishers much more easily than if I were to reach out on my own. And tracking the performance of those publishers is so simple. They make sending payments out to publishers a breeze. They have great API to handle lots of different types of transaction requests too. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex They also have an awesome team of employees across all departments. They now have a new tool to recruit affiliates, but from my experience, the tool is not as effective as working with an agency or attending conferences to meet new partners and expand.  Partnerize does not come with an account management team like some other networks, so be prepared to have your own team (in-house or outsourced) to manage publisher relationships. Their customer support and integrations teams are helpful and professional. I've experienced no outages or issues with accessing the platform or reports. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4147933 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize (Pz) manages all tracking, reporting, and invoicing for affiliates worldwide. There were many customizations we needed to the reporting and commissionable fields, which the Pz team were able to accommodate. The ability to commission on custom meta fields has allowed us to be more innovative with affiliate payout schemes. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle" 2.667z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="tag" data-container="body" title="Invitation from G2 on behalf of a seller or affiliate. This reviewer was offered a nominal incentive as thanks for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Review source: G2 invite on behalf of seller</div><div class="tag" title="This reviewer was offered a nominal incentive as thanks for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Incentivized Review</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-8"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2020-03-03" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2020-03-03">Mar 03, 2020</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/partnerize/reviews/partnerize-review-4137577"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Great platform overall"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize is a great platform for managing partners and our affiliate program. Where it shines is around the commissioning rules to commission on any meta parameter along with it's reporting and the ability to export every detail of an order to dive deeper into a partner's performance. As a SaaS platform, enhancements are always being worked on to improve usability and they take feedback from partners on what features are needed. Another reason we chose Partnerize was their ability to make payments to partners globally. Support is generally quite helpful in answering any questions within a reasonable time. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Some newly released enhancements to current tools lack features at the start that were available in the legacy version or can make the same process a bit more convoluted and I find myself using the legacy versions more when available. Since Partnerize is a SaaS platform, affiliate recruitment help will be limited and you'll need to rely mostly on the publisher recruitment tool itself. There's also no help with strategies in working with affiliates or insights into the market performance like with other networks. However, they do have a publisher recruitment team that will make intros to key partners they work with, but the rest is up to you. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4137577 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize was brought on to help grow the business and leverage affiliates/influencers to promote iHerb while earning a commission doing so. We've been able to control commission rates for low-value partners and increase commission rates for higher quality ones. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle" When there are issues, their team is readily available to help and strategize on how we can solve them through the tech platform.
